name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Selected Room
info:Stayed in September 2022
info:Friends
info:4 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted September 16, 2022
msg:Since I moved to a foreign country, the Internet has not been set up for a long time. I only come to comment now. I am very sorry. It is a bit long to write a travel note. I will first introduce the hotel and then praise the lovely Xiao Jiu!

"Anlu" is an exquisite Hui style hotel hidden near the ancient town of Zhujiajiao. ''An' means tranquility and stability, ''lu'' means a place of seclusion, and "An Yujian" expresses transparency, calmness and ease. The self-satisfied way of life seems to want to create a pure land of indifference and meditation for hermits.

The details of the hotel are inseparable from traditional cultural elements, such as ancient Huizhou architecture, Jiangnan gardens, bamboo forests and green plants, ancient furniture, piano, chess, calligraphy and painting, flower arrangement, tea ceremony experience, etc., full of ancient charm. 35 townhouse-style rooms, wooden structure and decoration, spacious and comfortable, each has a double-sided washbasin and an exclusive private garden, the scenery outside the window is exclusive, elegant and quiet; when the bed is opened in the evening, the housekeeper will provide according to the twenty-four solar terms. Tremella, longan and red dates soup is delivered to the room, which is intimate and warm. There are also all-day dining restaurants, snack bars, scholar pavilions, spas, indoor swimming pools... The facilities are complete; the lobby bar can freely experience piano, chess, calligraphy and painting, or change into Hanfu to feel the elegant and ancient style; the lobby looks up at the entire row on the second floor The wooden window, the former embroidered building, is now a scholarly pavilion for enjoying tea and reading; in addition, there is a special person to guide the historical sites every day, so that the accommodation tourists know why.

The exterior building of the hotel lobby has five rare pairs of crested heads. It is known as "the first official hall in the south of the Yangtze River" in the Ming Dynasty. come out in large numbers. The whole building follows the pattern of "front five and seven bays, three entrances and two patios". The iconic fire-proof and anti-theft horse head high wall restores the social microcosm of that era; there are ingot trays under the wax gourd beams, and corbels hanging upside down on the door lintels. , eaves column, bird for (mainly for load-bearing), next to the newly-made brick carved window lattice (the ancient residence can not be extended if broken). From the size of the house lion on the two sides, the official position of the original owner of the house can be judged. The disc "Mendang" at the main entrance represents the drum of war. It can be seen that the owner of the mansion is a military general, and the 9-inch threshold shows the owner's official position Chonglong (the same height as the threshold of the palace). After entering the door, the first courtyard is open, and the ground is paved with golden bricks (same as the Forbidden City). It takes three years for a "golden brick" to take three years from soil extraction to final formation, which is unimaginable. At night, the rose-red lanterns on the promenade on both sides of the patio smudge the extravagance of officials and officials.

The ancient stage opposite Wufeng Tower, originally built in the late Qing Dynasty, is also a Huizhou architecture with a history of more than 200 years (Anhui and Jiangxi belong to ancient Huizhou). It is a place for various social activities and opera halls. The first two perennial beautiful cherry trees, in the blooming season, use pink flower mist to set off the ancient stage with the gold picture on the black background. The four-clawed pythons, lions, Cao Cao's banquet, bronze sparrow stage, Guo Ziyi's birthday banquet, etc. carved on the eaves of the fourth floor are all allusions related to the stage; the paintings on the horse head wall next to the bat, magpie, elk, birds and beasts represent good fortune Full of blessings, good luck, and long-lasting descendants. The disk caisson in the middle of the roof, the main worshiper makes a sound, and the clouds on the beams and columns in front of the stage represent the blue sky.

At the beginning of the unblocking in June, I went to stay at the Prime Minister's Mansion Hotel in Guangfulin, which is also a historic site that was demolished and built. However, the Anlu Hotel is more open and a**ospheric, and the room design also continues the classical style of the Huizhou style of Daiwa and white walls, and the service details More active and subtle, the best thing is the special tour guide, which allows travelers to better understand the concept of the hotel and get closer to the charm and cultural heritage of ancient buildings.

 During this stay, I felt a lot about the hotel service. It really is "one person is enough to prosper the store, but it can also destroy the store"! My mother and I took taxis to the door of the hotel. My mother brought her little grandson, baby stroller and luggage, but no one helped to push the luggage. It really did not meet the basic standard of five-star; Outside, the welcome red dates and lotus leaf honey water was not delivered immediately, the service attitude was negligent and neglected, and the mother was extremely unhappy. After we came, we saw Xiao Jiu, our housekeeper, who immediately served tea, helped with luggage, etc. A little girl with a big temper.

After entering the room, I obviously felt that the air-conditioning was insufficient, and the musty smell was quite strong. After contacting Xiaojiu, the staff checked it two or three times. They all said that there was no problem with the air-conditioning. The height of the room is high and it takes time to cool down. Jiu also offered to help us change rooms, but declined because the child fell asleep. After dinner, Xiaojiu checked the air-conditioning supply again. It happened that the children also got up. Xiaojiu suggested to upgrade us to a new room and transfer us to the new room by a special car. During this period, the two staff helped us move a lot of things. Luggage (it's really a lot, we have seven big suitcases because we moved abroad), and the golf cart is full and moved three times! During this period, I apologized frequently for the inconvenience caused. The best thing is that the air-conditioning in the room has been adjusted to a comfortable temperature. It turns out that Xiaojiu prepared the room in advance after learning that the air-conditioning in our room would not come down, and the air-conditioning has been turned on! Having a caring butler is really important! Because it was more than ten o'clock after the luggage was moved the day before. Xiaojiu also offered to apply for a late check-out for us, so that we could finish our lunch in a hurry and then do the check-out procedure. The overall service is still a plus, thank you for the caring Xiaojiu!

msg:Stayed in so many hotels
I was deeply shocked by the hotel lobby for the first time

Wufeng Tower was originally a palace building. It was used by Huizhou architecture for the construction of ancestral hall gates during the Ming and Qing Dynasties. As the hotel lobby, Wufeng Tower was known as the "First Official Hall of the South of the Yangtze River", an ancient Huizhou building in Ming Dynasty. Covering an area of 1330 square meters, the first five and seven bays in the back, three entrances and two patios, hand-built, amazing scale, magnificent, and spacious, it is really a boutique Wufenglou that is hard to see in a century.

The owner of this residence, Mr. Qin Tongqian, is committed to rescuing and protecting ancient buildings. This building was discovered by Mr. Qin that it had been completely destroyed and collapsed at the beginning. It was carefully repaired and built by hundreds of national treasure-class ancient construction craftsmen. After five years, the ruins and broken bricks and tiles returned to flesh and blood. Zhujiajiao reappears majestic.

Room: The hall courtyard, antique, large bathing area, everywhere reflects a corner of the scene, even the soaking bathtub has vegetation design as the background. Snacks at the room bar are all free, and soup is delivered every day according to the twenty-four solar terms.

Breakfast: Set meals are available in 10 rooms or less. There are Chinese and Western styles to choose from. It is too rich. Two sets of meals can't be eaten by three people.

Activities: We prepared various activities such as ancient architecture explanation, calligraphy, painting, incense making and so on for the children. We participated in the Taiji morning exercises in the morning. The young lady who led the exercises is so awesome!

SPA: The price/performance ratio is really high! The SPA room is very comfortable and the technician‚Äôs technique is also great [Âº∫]

Surrounding: Zhujiajiao Ancient Town is a 10-minute walk away. It is quite beautiful at night. The ancient town is well-preserved and not over-commercialized. There are many residents. The living area of the original residents is more smoky than the commercial area.

The hotel‚Äôs butler service is very considerate. Xiao Liu, the butler, sends activity information the day before check-in, and a travel tea set when he leaves the store. What a pleasant surprise!

In short, it is a perfect hotel and experience. I have stayed in many hotels in China, and Hong Kong‚Äôs upper house is comparable. I will definitely come again in the future!
